about_this_resource_text: '<p>Prof. Szolovits gives an overview of clinical care from
  the past to the present. The main topics covered are the goals of medicine, the
  tasks of medicine, public health, and paying for health care.</p> <p>Speaker: Peter
  Szolovits</p>             <p><a href="./resolveuid/0ea60e881b96ffbc4896947d816bc434">Lecture
  2: Overview of Clinical Care slides (PDF - 3.9MB)</a></p>'

  <span m="1934550">these</span> <span m="1934760">diseases</span> <span m="1935390">in</span>
  <span m="1935510">the</span> <span m="1935570">first</span> <span m="1935870">place?</span>
  <span m="1936930">And</span> <span m="1936950">that's</span> <span m="1937370">sort</span>

  m="1939500">OK.</span> <span m="1941090">So</span> <span m="1941240">that's</span>
  <span m="1942200">about</span> <span m="1943190">what</span> <span m="1943460">medicine</span>
  <span m="1943970">tries</span> <span m="1944390">to</span> <span m="1944540">do.</span>
  <span m="1945440">But</span> <span m="1945650">how</span> <span m="1945830">does</span>
  <span m="1946010">it</span> <span m="1946100">do</span> <span m="1946400">it?</span>
  <span m="1946820">And</span> <span m="1946970">so</span> <span m="1947180">we're</span>
  <span m="1947300">going</span> <span m="1947450">to</span> <span m="1947510">talk</span>
  <span m="1947810">a</span> <span m="1947870">little</span> <span m="1948080">bit</span>
  <span m="1948830">about</span> <span m="1949160">the</span> <span m="1949280">traditional</span>
  <span m="1949910">tasks</span> <span m="1950630">that</span> <span m="1950810">are</span>
  <span m="1950960">attributed</span> <span m="1952340">to</span> <span m="1952520">health</span>

  <span m="1960110">diagnosis--</span> <span m="1961160">I</span> <span m="1961280">go</span>
  <span m="1961430">to</span> <span m="1961520">my</span> <span m="1961700">doctor.</span>
  <span m="1962390">I</span> <span m="1962570">say,</span> <span m="1962840">doc,</span>

  <span m="1964340">horrible</span> <span m="1964760">headache.</span> <span m="1965210">I've</span>
  <span m="1965390">had</span> <span m="1965600">it</span> <span m="1965720">for</span>
  <span m="1965900">two</span> <span m="1966110">weeks.</span> <span m="1967460">What's</span>
  <span m="1967700">wrong</span> <span m="1967970">with</span> <span m="1968150">me?</span>
  <span m="1970340">And</span> <span m="1970670">his</span> <span m="1970940">job--</span>
  <span m="1973380">in</span> <span m="1973500">my</span> <span m="1973710">case,</span>
  <span m="1974170">it</span> <span m="1974190">happens</span> <span m="1974610">to</span>

  <span m="1977730">to</span> <span m="1979230">come</span> <span m="1979470">up</span>
  <span m="1979620">with</span> <span m="1979800">an</span> <span m="1979920">answer.</span>

  <span m="1981270">me?</span></p><p><span m="1984340">Prognosis</span> <span m="1986110">is</span>

  <span m="1995030">is</span> <span m="1995240">this</span> <span m="1995450">headache</span>

  <span m="2192940">what</span> <span m="2193150">to</span> <span m="2193270">do</span>

  <span m="2452370">diagnosis.</span> <span m="2453750">From</span> <span m="2454080">the</span>
  <span m="2454230">initial</span> <span m="2454680">complaints,</span> <span m="2455670">guess</span>
  <span m="2456060">a</span> <span m="2456120">suitable</span> <span m="2456630">hypothesis.</span>
  <span m="2459240">Use</span> <span m="2459750">the</span> <span m="2459900">current</span>
  <span m="2460440">active</span> <span m="2460920">hypotheses</span> <span m="2461850">to</span>
  <span m="2462000">guide</span> <span m="2462330">questioning--</span> <span m="2463710">so</span>
  <span m="2463950">to</span> <span m="2464130">order</span> <span m="2464430">more</span>
  <span m="2464670">tests,</span> <span m="2465270">to</span> <span m="2465390">ask</span>
  <span m="2465660">questions</span> <span m="2466230">of</span> <span m="2466350">the</span>
  <span m="2466440">patient.</span> <span m="2468430">And</span> <span m="2468640">it's</span>
  <span m="2468850">the</span> <span m="2468970">failure</span> <span m="2469570">to</span>
  <span m="2469750">satisfy</span> <span m="2470410">expectations</span> <span m="2471460">that's</span>
  <span m="2471760">the</span> <span m="2471880">strongest</span> <span m="2472570">clue</span>
  <span m="2473530">to</span> <span m="2473710">how</span> <span m="2473890">to</span>
  <span m="2473980">develop</span> <span m="2474460">a</span> <span m="2474520">better</span>
  <span m="2474820">hypothesis.</span></p><p><span m="2478540">And</span> <span m="2478660">then</span>

  <span m="2980770">people</span> <span m="2981190">do.</span> <span m="2982430">And</span>

  <span m="2984640">happens</span> <span m="2985180">to</span> <span m="2985330">those</span>

  <span m="3243200">that</span> <span m="3243920">in</span> <span m="3244070">this</span>
  <span m="3244280">course.</span></p><p><span m="3245990">OK,</span> <span m="3248010">the</span>
  <span m="3248220">other</span> <span m="3248430">thing</span> <span m="3248940">that</span>
  <span m="3249180">medicine</span> <span m="3249660">tries</span> <span m="3250020">to</span>

  <span m="3536740">have</span> <span m="3537010">ICD-9</span> <span m="3537820">CM</span>

  <span m="4624540">a</span> <span m="4624930">hospital</span> <span m="4625470">readmission</span>

  <span m="4635220">hospital</span> <span m="4636210">and</span> <span m="4636390">you're</span>

  <span m="4644330">that</span> <span m="4644570">readmission,</span> <span m="4645260">or</span>
  <span m="4645380">not</span> <span m="4645590">pay</span> <span m="4645800">you</span>
